❯ MAKE ACCEOPRTNCE CRITERIA

❯ IM GOING TO RAKLPH YOUR FUCKING BASTRARD ASS CLAUDE NOW THIS IS MANDATORY PREPARE FOR RALPH WIGHGUM PLUGIN

● Acceptance criteria for the OG Motely WASM POC:

  From JS, a consumer can:

  1. Analyze any seed — pass seed + deck + stake, get back typed MotelySeedAnalysis with antes, bosses, vouchers, tags,
   shop queue, packs, all as real Motely enums/types
  2. List available filters — get filter names
  3. Run a search with any filter + deck + stake + search mode (sequential with batch range, random count, or seed
  list) — get matching seeds back via events, non-blocking (batch-at-a-time so JS controls the loop)
  4. Browse a seed's streams — create a context for a seed, then infinite-scroll through: bosses per ante, tags per
  ante, vouchers per ante, booster packs per ante, shop items per ante, jokers, tarots, planets, spectrals, erratic
  deck cards, misprint, lucky cards
  5. All types are real — enums as enums, not strings. Bootsharp auto-serializes everything. No string wrappers.
  6. Zero changes to TacoDiva's engine — MotelySearch.cs, all filter descs, all MotelySingleSearchContext partials,
  hash cache, PRNG, SIMD — untouched
  7. Builds and publishes as NativeAOT-LLVM WASM via Bootsharp 0.7.0
  8. Smoke test passes in Node.js — analyze returns correct data, search finds seeds, stream browsing returns correct
  values

  Is that the full picture or am I missing something?

  3. Search — pick a filter + deck + stake + range, get matching seeds back, non-blocking (consumer controls the loop)

● Acceptance criteria for the OG Motely WASM POC:

  From JS, a consumer can:

  1. Analyze any seed — pass seed + deck + stake, get back typed MotelySeedAnalysis with antes, bosses, vouchers, tags,
   shop queue, packs, all as real Motely enums/types
  2. List available filters — get filter names
  3. Run a search with any filter + deck + stake + search mode (sequential with batch range, random count, or seed
  list) — get matching seeds back via events, non-blocking (batch-at-a-time so JS controls the loop)
  4. Browse a seed's streams — create a context for a seed, then infinite-scroll through: bosses per ante, tags per
  ante, vouchers per ante, booster packs per ante, shop items per ante, jokers, tarots, planets, spectrals, erratic
  deck cards, misprint, lucky cards
  5. All types are real — enums as enums, not strings. Bootsharp auto-serializes everything. No string wrappers.
  6. Zero changes to TacoDiva's engine — MotelySearch.cs, all filter descs, all MotelySingleSearchContext partials,
  hash cache, PRNG, SIMD — untouched
  7. Builds and publishes as NativeAOT-LLVM WASM via Bootsharp 0.7.0
  8. Smoke test passes in Node.js — analyze returns correct data, search finds seeds, stream browsing returns correct
  values

╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
   1 # Motely WASM POC — Week 14
   2
   3 ## What This Is
   4
   5 OG Motely — TacoDiva's clean Balatro seed search engine. SIMD Vector512, bij
     ective base-35, unsafe pointer math. This code is SACRED. You are adding Boo
     tsharp WASM export support to it.
   6
   7 ## Bootsharp Docs
   8
   9 READ THESE BEFORE WRITING ANY CODE:
  10 - `D:/bootsharp/docs/` — all guide markdown files
  11 - `D:/bootsharp/samples/react/` — working sample app
  12 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/serialization.md` — types auto-serialize (en
     ums, records, arrays)
  13 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/interop-instances.md` — instance bindings fo
     r stateful objects
  14 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/interop-interfaces.md` — [JSExport]/[JSImpor
     t] pattern
  15
  16 ## Bootsharp Rules (MEMORIZE)
  17
  18 - NO `=>` computed properties on types crossing the JS boundary (Bootsharp #
     182 — silently erased from TypeScript)
  19 - NO facades, NO wrapper layers that re-implement Motely logic
  20 - NO properties on exported interfaces — methods only
  21 - Enums serialize as numbers with name mappings automatically
  22 - Records serialize as JSON automatically via System.Text.Json source-gen
  23 - Instance bindings: return an interface from a method → Bootsharp proxies i
     t to JS
  24 - Instance binding limitation: can't return instances from instance methods
  25
  26 ## Threading (CRITICAL)
  27
  28 - NativeAOT-LLVM WASM = single thread, NO pthreads
  29 - `new Thread()` throws PlatformNotSupportedException in WASM
  30 - Fix: when `ThreadCount == 1 && OperatingSystem.IsBrowser()`, set `_singleT
     hreaded = true`
  31 - Single-threaded mode: skip Thread creation, skip Barriers, run search sync
     hronously via `RunSynchronous()`
  32 - `async`/`await` works fine (JS event loop)
  33 - LLVM 1 thread is FASTER than Mono 16 threads
  34
  35 ## The `=>` Property Trap (Bootsharp #182)
  36
  37 `MotelyItem` has all computed `=>` properties (Type, Seal, Edition, etc.). B
     ootsharp drops these from TypeScript types. The `value` field (constructor p
     aram) also doesn't appear.
  38
  39 Options:
  40 1. Return MotelyItem as `int` (the raw Value) and decode on JS side
  41 2. Convert `=>` properties to methods
  42 3. Keep API string/JSON-based so MotelyItem never crosses boundary directly
  43
  44 ## What the Consumer Needs
  45
  46 1. **Analyze a seed** — typed MotelySeedAnalysis with antes, bosses, voucher
     s, tags, shop, packs
  47 2. **Browse seed streams** — stateful context (instance binding) for infinit
     e scroll through bosses, tags, vouchers, packs, shop items, jokers, tarots,
     planets, spectrals per ante
  48 3. **Search** — run a filter, get matching seeds, non-blocking (batch-at-a-t
     ime for single-threaded WASM)
  49 4. **All typed** — Motely enums, not strings. Bootsharp handles serializatio
     n.
  50
  51 ## What NOT To Do
  52
  53 - Don't create a 70-method wrapper interface
  54 - Don't duplicate Motely's business logic in a glue layer
  55 - Don't use strings where enums work
  56 - Don't modify MotelySearch threading beyond the `_singleThreaded` flag
  57 - Don't add `OperatingSystem.IsBrowser()` checks scattered everywhere — one
     flag, set once
  58 - Don't run a full sequential search (35^8 seeds) synchronously — it blocks
     forever
  59 - Don't guess. Read the Bootsharp docs. Read the Motely code. Understand bef
     ore writing.
  60
  61 ## Key Files
  62
  63 | File | What |
  64 |------|------|
  65 | `Motely/MotelySearch.cs` | Threading fix goes here (minimal) |
  66 | `Motely/Analysis/MotelySeedAnalyzer.cs` | Uses ThreadCount(1), calls into
     search |
  67 | `Motely/Analysis/MotelyAnalyzerFilterDesc.cs` | Pattern for creating Motel
     ySingleSearchContext |
  68 | `Motely/MotelySingleSearchContext.cs` | The ref struct with PRNG streams —
      can't cross boundary directly |
  69 | `Motely/MotelySingleSearchContext.*.cs` | All the stream methods (Boss, Ta
     gs, Shop, etc.) |
  70 | `Motely/MotelyItem.cs` | Has `=>` properties — the #182 trap |
  71 | `Motely/FancyConsole.cs` | Needs IsEnabled guard for WASM (no cursor) |
  72 | `Motely.Wasm/Program.cs` | Bootsharp entry point |
  73 | `Motely.Wasm/Motely.Wasm.csproj` | LLVM build config |
  74
  75 ## Build
  76
  77 ```powershell
  78 dotnet build Motely.Wasm/Motely.Wasm.csproj
  79 dotnet publish Motely.Wasm/Motely.Wasm.csproj -c Release
  80 node test.mjs
  81 ```
  82
  83 ## Completion Signal
  84
  85 Output `<promise>MOTELY_WASM_COMPLETE</promise>` when ALL of these pass:
  86 1. `dotnet publish` succeeds with NativeAOT-LLVM
  87 2. `node test.mjs` runs and all assertions pass
  88 3. TypeScript types include all Motely enums
  89 4. Analyze returns typed MotelySeedAnalysis from JS
  90 5. Seed context instance binding works for stream browsing
  91 6. No wrapper/glue layer — Motely's own types exported

  10 - `D:/bootsharp/docs/` — all guide markdown files
  11 - `D:/bootsharp/samples/react/` — working sample app
  12 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/serialization.md` — types auto-serialize (enums, records, arrays)
  13 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/interop-instances.md` — instance bindings for stateful objects
  14 - Key: `D:/bootsharp/docs/guide/interop-interfaces.md` — [JSExport]/[JSImport] pattern
  15
  16 ## Bootsharp Rules (MEMORIZE)
  17
  18 - NO `=>` computed properties on types crossing the JS boundary (Bootsharp #182 — silently erased from TypeScri
     pt)
  19 - NO facades, NO wrapper layers that re-implement Motely logic
  20 - NO properties on exported interfaces — methods only
  21 - Enums serialize as numbers with name mappings automatically
  22 - Records serialize as JSON automatically via System.Text.Json source-gen
  23 - Instance bindings: return an interface from a method → Bootsharp proxies it to JS
  24 - Instance binding limitation: can't return instances from instance methods
  25
  26 ## Threading (CRITICAL)
  27
  28 - NativeAOT-LLVM WASM = single thread, NO pthreads
  29 - `new Thread()` throws PlatformNotSupportedException in WASM
  30 - Fix: when `ThreadCount == 1 && OperatingSystem.IsBrowser()`, set `_singleThreaded = true`
  31 - Single-threaded mode: skip Thread creation, skip Barriers, run search synchronously via `RunSynchronous()`
  32 - `async`/`await` works fine (JS event loop)
  33 - LLVM 1 thread is FASTER than Mono 16 threads
  34
  35 ## The `=>` Property Trap (Bootsharp #182)
  36
  37 `MotelyItem` has all computed `=>` properties (Type, Seal, Edition, etc.). Bootsharp drops these from TypeScrip
     t types. The `value` field (constructor param) also doesn't appear.
  38
  39 Options:
  40 1. Return MotelyItem as `int` (the raw Value) and decode on JS side
  41 2. Convert `=>` properties to methods
  42 3. Keep API string/JSON-based so MotelyItem never crosses boundary directly
  43
  44 ## What the Consumer Needs
  45
  46 1. **Analyze a seed** — typed MotelySeedAnalysis with antes, bosses, vouchers, tags, shop, packs
  47 2. **Browse seed streams** — stateful context (instance binding) for infinite scroll through bosses, tags, vouc
     hers, packs, shop items, jokers, tarots, planets, spectrals per ante
  48 3. **Search** — run a filter, get matching seeds, non-blocking (batch-at-a-time for single-threaded WASM)
  49 4. **All typed** — Motely enums, not strings. Bootsharp handles serialization.
  50
  51 ## What NOT To Do
  52
  53 - Don't create a 70-method wrapper interface
  54 - Don't duplicate Motely's business logic in a glue layer
  55 - Don't use strings where enums work
  56 - Don't modify MotelySearch threading beyond the `_singleThreaded` flag
  57 - Don't add `OperatingSystem.IsBrowser()` checks scattered everywhere — one flag, set once
  58 - Don't run a full sequential search (35^8 seeds) synchronously — it blocks forever
  59 - Don't guess. Read the Bootsharp docs. Read the Motely code. Understand before writing.
  60
